 jediu kaa kahana tha ki yah koun si nai parampara kii ham shuruyaat karne ja rahe hai jahaan ek baar raashtrapati banane ke 5 saal baad phir usee vyakti ke naam par vichaar kiya ja rahaa he
 This has not happened in the country yet
 baithak main kaha gaya ki pranab mukherjee ko keval sonia gandhi kaa ummidavaar na maanakar sabakaa ummidavaar bana diya jaae kyonki unke kad or unke raajnneetik anubhav par kisi ko koi andeh nahin hona chahie
 But it did not work
 bal thakare pehle hi 'saamana' main pranab mukherjee ko samarthan de chuke the or ab jediu bhi alag ho gai
 Now consider the warm relations between Nitish and Narendra Modi
 
 
 yaad kiijie 2009 ke chunaav prachaar kaa antim din
 All the big leaders gathered in NDA rally in Ludhiana, Modi and Nitish too
 nitish kumaar modi se najar bachaa rahe the lekin modi bhi tehre khilaadi khud chalakar niteesha ke paas pahunche, gale mili or haath milaayaa
 But the cracks in this picture were seen when on the first day of the BJP executive meeting in Patna, a newspaper was published in Bihar newspapers mentioning how Gujarat helped Bihar during the Kosi floods
 iske baad nitish kumaar bhadak gaye
 Nitish Kumar immediately asked this poster to remove his picture
 yahi nahin, kosi kii madad ke naam par mili rakam gujarat sarkaar ko waapas kar di
 And the feast in honor of the BJP executive was also canceled
 darasal nitish ko maaloom he ki bihar main atipichhadon, mahadaliton or alpsankhyakon ke saath pichhadon kaa jo gathjod unki raajnneeti ko takat de rahaa he usamen modi se unki qareebi daraar daal sakati he
 Therefore, he does not allow any such opportunity in which he appears to be different and disagreeing with Modi
 haal hi main jab modi ne bihar kii jativaadee raajnneeti kaa zikr kiya to nitish ne taana maaraa ki modi gujarat kii chintaa karen, bihar kii nahin
 The comments yahi nahin, haal main hi ek angreji patrika main nitish sarkaar par ek visheshank aayaa jisamen unki sarkaar kii aalochana kii gai thi
 Nitish Kumar is also unhappy that an appendix containing a 16-page advertisement of the Gujarat government is also printed in the same magazine
 nitish ke najdiki isamen bhi modi kaa haath dekh rahe hai
 By the way, Nitish knows that a section of BJP suddenly becomes sensitive on Modi's question and such elements are active in his government as well
 unki hi sarkaar ke ek mantri ne modi ke haq main bayaan dene shuru kar die
 However, JDU is fully with them on this issue
 jaahir he niteesha apana kad badhaane or rashtriya raajnneeti main apni ek ahm bhoomika bhi chaahate hai
 But is he coming close to the UPA on the same excuse
 
 
 philhal yah kahana thodi jaldbaaji hogi kyonki abhi tak yah nahin pataa ki badale main kendra se unhen kya milegaa
 The law and order in Bihar has been fixed, the migration of people has also reduced but the power problem is serious there and now the patience of the people is getting broken
 modi ne bijepi par apana dabadabaa kaayam rakhaa he
 
 
 Sanjay Joshi had to withdraw
 adwani or sushamaa ne apane aap ko kinare kar liya
 Nitish knows that Sangma's name for the presidency was proposed by Jayalalitha, who is very close to Narendra Modi
 yahi vajah he ki jediu sangama ke naam par bidak gaya
 Even Nitish did not pick up Sangma's phone
 nitish ko yah bhi pataa he ki bhale hi modi abhi becoground main hon lekin 2014 ke chunaav kii asli kaman unheen ke haath main rahegi
 Nitish seems to have decided to end the JDU and BJP alliance in Bihar just before the Gujarat elections
 yahi vajah he ki nitish ne shivanand tiwari ko endie kii baithak main sa taur par dilli bheja
 Perhaps Nitish would not have been so confident of Sharad Yadav
 baithak main shivanand tiwari ne pranab da kaa paksh liya lekin sushamaa swaraj adi raheen
 Sushma referred to the meeting of Advani and Jayalalithaa and talked about contesting elections
 bijepi ko abhi tak kalam ke haa kehane kii ummid thi
 JDU said which new tradition are we going to start where once after 5 years of becoming President, the name of the same person is being considered
 abhi tak desh main aisa hua nahin he
 It was said in the meeting that Pranab Mukherjee should not be considered the candidate of Sonia Gandhi, because no one should have any doubt on his stature and his political experience
 lekin, baat nahin bani
 Bal Thackeray had already supported Pranab Mukherjee in 'saamana' and now JDU also split
 ab jaraa nitish or narendra modi ke naram−garam rishton par gaur karen
 
 
 Remember the last day of the 2009 election campaign
 ludhiana main endie kii raily main sabhi bade netaa jute modi bhi or nitish bhi
 Nitish Kumar was keeping an eye out for Modi, but even the stalled players themselves came to Nitish, hugged and shook hands
 magar is tasviir main daraar us vakt dikhi jab patna main bijepi kii kaaryakarini kii baithak ke pehle din bihar ke akhabaaron main ek ishtehaar chapa jisamen is baat kaa bhi zikr kiya gaya ki kis tarah gujarat ne kosi kii baadh ke vakt bihar kii madad kii
 After this, Nitish Kumar erupted
 nitish kumaar ne fouran is poster se apni tasviir hataane ke liye kaha
 Not only this, the money received in the name of Kosi's help was returned to the Gujarat government
 or bijepi kii kaaryakarini ke sammaan main di jane vaali daavat bhi radd kar di
 In fact, Nitish knows that in Bihar, the backward alliances with the backward castes, Mahadalits and minorities are giving strength to their politics, their close rift with Modi
 isliye vah aisa koi mauka jane nahin dete jisamen vah modi se alag or asahmat hote dikhen
 Recently, when Modi mentioned the casteist politics of Bihar, Nitish taunted that Modi should worry about Gujarat and not Bihar
 tippaniyan Not only this, a special issue came out recently on Nitish Sarkar in an English magazine in which his government was criticized
 nitish kumaar isse bhi khafa hai ki usee patrika main gujarat sarkaar kaa 16 pej kaa vigyaapan vaala ek parishisht bhi chapa he
 Modi's hand is also seen in this close to Nitish
 vaise nitish ko andaaza he ki modi ke sawaal par bijepi kaa ek hissaa achaanak samvedansheel ho uthta he or aise tatv unki sarkaar main bhi sakriy hai
 a minister in his own government started making statements in favor of Modi
 haalanki jediu is masale par puri tarah unke saath he
 Obviously, Nitish wants to increase his stature and also play an important role in national politics
 lekin kya isi bahaane vah upie ke najadik aa rahe hai

 xxrep 8 ? # Repost @officialhumansofbombay “I was born in the small town of Gwalior
 My parents were in d medical field & i was going to do engineering
 But in 9th grade, i saw Baazigar & i knew i wanted to be on the other side of the screen
 i was unsure of my parents' reaction — so i decided to study till 12th in Gwalior & den go to college in Mumbai
 Luckily i got into a college in Navi Mumbai
 i stayed in a hostel & searched for auditions
 i had no contacts,so I'd type keywords like, ‘actor Needed' on Facebook
 I'd travel for 6 hours 3-4 times a week for auditions
 At times, I'd be rejected from outside the studio because i didn't ‘look the part'
 But i still had hope
 Soon i got projects like a few seconds in an ad & they kept me going
 Served i rented a flat in Andheri with 12 boys
 i had limited finances
 i couldn't even afford a portfolio — I'd crop my face out of group photos to send to agents! All the while I'd skip college to give auditions & my parents didn't know about any of this
 Once i saw an ad for a film audition & decided to go for it
 They liked me & auditioned me many times
 My final audition script was the monologue that then became my identity! Finally, when i got the role, i was at Andheri station & immediately called my mom! She couldn't believe it! After 2 & a half years of struggle, what i had imagined as a possibility, was now a reality
 After Pyaar Ka Punchama, there are still many opportunities
 i stayed in the same flat with 12 boys till my third film! At the time, my mom was adamant i finish my degree, so while shooting, i gave my exams—& people in the exam hall were clicking photos with me! But i understood that she wanted my future to be secure
 After Sonu Ke Titu Ki Sweety, it all changed! Life has come full circle now — recently when i was in Gwalior, i was invited to my school as chief guest & kids were chanting my name! It was surreal! But what i have today, would've never come my way, if i hadn't believed that I'd make it
 I'm grateful for where i am & i know i have a long way to go
 Sometimes all of it still feels unbelievable from this point on, the possibilities just seem endless & my dreams, r just waiting to come true

 bharat kii yatra par haal main aae america suraksha salaahkaar ne pakistan ko paroksh yuddh band karne kii naseehat di thi
 On Wednesday, US MP and Speaker of the House Democratic Caucus Joe Crowley warned Pakistan that it would not sit silent if attacks on India's troops and its civilians continued
 iske saath hi unhone islamabad se uski jameen par sakriya kattarpanthi takaton par karrwai karne kii maang kii he
 Crowley demanded the Donald Trump government put more pressure on Pakistan in this matter
 south africa cricket team ke purv captain greem smithne apni patni se alag hone kaa faisla kar liya he
 Smith was married to Irish model Morgan Dean three and a half years ago
 danpati ke vakil david baker ne media se kaha, ‘main pushti karata hum ki greem or morgan durbhaagya se talaak le rahe hai
 This is clearly a personal matter and the couple wants their privacy to be respected during this time
 ’is danpati kii ek beti or ek betaa hai
 On 25 July 2012, Morgan gave birth to Christine while on 15 July 2013 she gave birth to mcmorin
 smith kii beti badi he jabaki mecmoris usase ek saal chota he
 Under the captaincy of Smith, the South African cricket team won the ICC Test 'mace'
 smith ne dakshin africa ke liye 117 test match khele hai or 2014 main paariwarik jimmedaariyon kaa hawala dete hue unhone sanyas le liya tha
 'how dare you play with my son
 tumhen nahin pataa ki tum kya ho or kahaan se aate ho? pard-likhakar zyada se zyada apane pita kaa kaam karke thodaa paisa kama logo, tum kitna bhi pard loge rahoge to rickshaw hi chalaane vaale' ye kuch aise shabd the jise sunakar-sunakar govind jaiswal bade hue the
 Hearing such words for himself, he always thought that how should he do such that people start respecting him
 unhone izzat paane ke liye padhai ko chunaa kyonki vah jaanate the ki padhai ke alaava koi bhi duusari cheez unhen in shabdon se chhutkaaraa nahin dilaa sakati he
 Who is Govind Jaiswal In his first attempt, Govind Jaiswal secured 48th rank in the 2006 IAS Examination
 hindi madhyam se pariksha dene waalon kii shrenee main vah topper rahe the
 Govind, 32, is currently the District Magistrate of the East Delhi Area
 govind ke pita narayan jaiswal padhe-likhe nahin hai or rickshaw chalaate hai
 He cannot even hear properly
 bete ke IAS banane ke sapane ko sirf khet bechakar hi puraa kiya ja saktaa tha
 His father sold the farm to send Govind to Delhi, but still could not meet the entire expenses of studies
 govind ne apana kharchaa chalaane ke liye bacchon ko ganit kitutionapadhaanaa shuru kii
 Govindalgaatar used to study for 18 hours while preparing for the exam and did not even eat food many times to save money
 bure din sikhaate hai sabaipane sangharsh ke bare main vah bataate hai, 'meri paristhatiyaan aisi thim ki civil sarvice kii taiyaari ke alaava mere paas koi chaara nahin tha
 Government jobs are mostly fixed, so they did not have opportunities for me
 na hi mere paas kaaphi rupee the jisase main bijness shuru kar sakuun
 The only thing i could do in this situation was to study a lot
 'rigelt aane se pehlekai dinon tak unke pita chintaa ke kaaran so nahin paae the
 When the result came, everyone had tears in their eyes
 govind apane safalataa kaa shrey apane pita or apni bahanon ko dete hai
 Especially the elder sister who left her studies to take care of the family members after the mother's death
 apane sangharsh ke dinon ke bare main unka kahana he ki agar wo bure din nahin hote to vah safalataa or jindagi kaa matlab kabhi samaj nahin pate
 The Supreme Court's decision on triple talaq is being welcomed by all political parties
 kendriya vitt mantri arun jetali ne is faisle ko aitihaasik bataaya he
 At the same time, Bahujan Samaj Party supremo Mayawati has also welcomed this decision
 yah faisla badi jeet or swaagatyogy kadam: arun jetalivitt or raksha mantri arun jetali ne kaha, 'supreme court kaa faisla un sabhi kii jeet he jo yah maanate the ki personal lau ko pragatisheel hona chahie or sanvaidhanik guarantee ke anuroop hona chahie
 This is a big win and a welcome move
 'bispi ne kiya faisle kaa svaagatbahujan samaaj party kii supremeo mayawati ne kaha, 'bispi faisle kaa swaagat karti he
 It would have been nice if the Muslim Personal Law Board had taken action in the triple divorce case itself, but they did not
 'aitihaasik faisla: ravishankar prasadkanoon mantri ravishankar prasad ne faisle kaa swaagat karte hue kaha, 'ye aitihaasik faisalaa he, jo supreme court ke bahumat se hua faisalaa he
 Woman power and greetings to Muslim sisters
 
 
 badlaav ho rahaa he

 duniya ke 22 deshon ne teen talaak ko band kiya he

 ye sarkaar rajeev gandhi kii sarkaar nahin he, ye modi ji sarkaar hai, jo kisi ke saamne nahin jhukegi
 Welcome Supreme Court verdict: Sushil Modibihar Deputy Chief Minister Sushil Kumar Modi has said that today the decision given by the Supreme Court on the issue of triple talaq is historic and we welcome this decision on our behalf
 unhone kaha, 'bijepi kii ye pehle se maang rahi he ki tripal talaak asanvaidhanik he, ye mahilaon kii garima ke khilaaf he, ye mahilaon ke prati anyaay he
 'this decision for a progressive and better future: Sachin Pilot, State President of Rajasthan Congress, Sachin Pilot has said that we respect the Supreme Court's decision on triple talaq, it is a commendable decision for a progressive country
 ye faisla desh hit main he
 He said that the government should enact a good law in Parliament, respecting the sentiments of all people
 jisamen sabake liye acha ho
 Pilot took credit for this decision to the BJP and said that we should not see everything through the eyes of politics
 aaj aitihaasik din: swati maliwaldillimhila ayogki adhyaksh swati maliwal ne tripal talaak ke faisle ko aitihaasik bataaya
 He said that this day will be written in history
 unhone kaha, 'quran main yah kahin nahin he ki koi jab chaahe kahin bhi apni patni ko talaak de de
 i am very happy with this decision
 ' The Election Commission has prepared a list of 200 such political parties, which are only on paper
 ayog inaki manyata radd karegaa
 The commission fears that these parties are being used for money laundering, so it will also send information about them to the Income Tax Department so that it can take further action
 indian express kii khabar ke anusaar manyata radd hone vaali partiyon ke bare main jaankaree aage kii karrwai ke liye chunaav ayog agle kuch hi dinon main kendriya pratyaksh kar board (cbdt)ko bhejega
 These are political parties who have not contested any elections since 2005 and their existence is merely on paper
 chunaav ayog ke adhikariyon ko andeshaa he ki aise kai raajnneetik dalon kaa istemaalamani londeringke liye ho rahaa he
 Officials say that this is just the beginning, after which the Election Commission will take action against all serious political parties
 aise kai raajnneetik dal inakam tex ritern daakhil nahin karte or karte bhi honge to uski copy chunaav ayog ko nahin bhejte
 The CBDT is being informed about this so that it can investigate the type of financial transactions done by these parties and eliminate the tax benefit to them
 chunaav ayog ko lagata he ki is tarah kii sakhti se aise log hatotsahit honge jo raajnneetik dal kaa gathan sirf kaale dhan ko safed karne ke liye karte hai
 According to Election Commission data, at present there are seven national political parties, 58 regional parties and other 1786 registered parties which have no identity
 aise agambhir raajnneetik dalon kaa chalan band karne ke liye saal 2004 main tatkaaleen mukhya chunaav ayukta ties krishnamurthi ne pradhanmantri ko patr bhi likhaa tha
 The Election Commission recommended that political parties give a record of all their donations, even if the amount is less than Rs 20,000, but this suggestion has not been implemented yet
 maujuuda kanoon ke mutabik sabhi raajnneetik dalon ko apane inakam tex ritern main sirf 20,000 rupye se upar kii raashi kaa hi strot bataanaa hota he
 Taking advantage of this, political parties show most of their donations for less than Rs
 20,000 and thus they do not have to disclose its source
 saal 1984 ke sikh danga maamle main cese ko dobaaraa shuru karne ke aadesh ke baad guuruuvaar ko hai court ne is maamle main sibiai ko notice diya he
 In fact, the court feels that despite having witnesses in the case, they were prevented from coming to the court and the Delhi Police neither conducted the investigation properly nor did any effort to get the culprits punished in the court
 police kii koshish in keson ko jald se jald court se khatm karne main dikhi
 During the hearing, the court has also released the production warrant of Balwant Khokhar, the accused in the case and the bandh in Tihar
 hai court maamle kii agali sunwaayee 1 may ko karegaa
 Significantly, last month, the Delhi High Court, while giving an important verdict, ordered the re-investigation of five cases related to the 1984 riots
 in sabhi maamalon ko 1986 main band kar diya gaya tha
 Among them, Sajjan Kumar, Balwan Khokhar, Mahendra Yadav, Krishna Khokhar are accused
 yah yachika sibiai kii taraf se daayar kii gayi thi
 The petition challenged the acquittal of Sajjan Kumar and the rest of the accused in 1986 charge sheets 10, 11, 31, 32 and 33
 hycourt ne in paanch maamalon kii jaanch main kii gai karmiyon par swat: sangyaan lete hue kaha ki in maamalon main pramukh chashmadid gavaahon se poochtacha hi nahin kii gai he
 This is a very funny thing
 hai court ne kaha ki maamalon ko badi jaldi main band kiya gaya, jisase aisa lagata he ki inamen sahi jaanch or trial hua hi nahin
 In this case, an order is ordered to be re-examined in all five cases
 isse pehle hai court nedilli puliceor sibiai se in maamalon ke record khojane kaa nirdesh diya tha, lekin jab record nahin mila to hai court ne in maamalon kii phir se jaanch karne kaa aadesh diya he
 Apart from this, the High Court has issued show cause notice to all the accused including Sajjan Kumar and sought answers
 hai court ne aropiyon se poocha he ki vah bataaen kii is maamle main dobaaraa jaanch kyon na shuru kii jaae

 Every married couple dreams of a successful marriage
 lekin kai baar jane-anjaane kai aisi galtiyaan karne se aapkaa yah sapana pal bhar main tut saktaa he
 a successful marriage can make all other relationships related to your life perfect
 haalanki shaadishuda jindagi ko hameshaa khushhaal banaae rakhana koi aasaan kaam nahin he
 For this, men should change their 5 habits which can cause a rift in their relationship
 aaie jaanate hai aakhir kya hai wo 5 aadaten
 Take care of time
 Even if you spend hours with your friends before marriage, but now doing so can upset your wife
 apane samay ko vyavasthit karen, doston ke liye samay nikaalte samay patni ko bhi quality time dena na bhoolen
 Help in household work by putting the responsibility of all the household work on the wife, she may not be able to take proper time for you
 aise main apane rishte ko thodaa romantic or majboot banane ke liye thode udaar banakar partner kii kichan main madad kar den
 Believe that by doing this, you will get more respect for them in their eyes
 tarif karnaa na bhuulenshadi hote hi zyaadaatar purush, apni patniyon kii tarif karnaa band kar dete hai
 Due to which many times their relationship starts getting boring
 aise main apane partner ko khaas mahasoos karwaane ke liye mauka pate hi jhat se unhen tarif main do shabd bol den
 By doing this your wife will feel good and their confidence will also increase
 impress karne kaa koi mauka nahin chodeshadi karne kaa matlab yah nahin he ki aap apane partner ko impress karnaa hi chhod den
 If you want to have a romance like the first day in love, then after marriage, make them feel special from time to time
 kabhi unke baithne ke liye kursi khinch den to kabhi unke liye pehle kii tarah car kaa darwaja kholen
 By doing this your wife will never feel that you no longer love them as before
 duusare ko sammaan na denaakai purushon ko lagata he ki unke nirnay sahi ho yaa galat lekin jeevanasathi hone ke naate unke partner ko unki har baat manani chahie
 Such people want to take all the decisions related to life themselves
